1b1(rgyud): rgyu ga skad du/ sar+b+ba ta thA ga tAtwAt+tA sam gra ha nA ma ma hA na hA
1b2(rgyud): bod skad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de khon nyid bsdus pa zhes bya ba thigs
1b3(rgyud): chen po'i mdo// bam po dang po/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag/ 
1b4(rgyud): 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdza/ 
1b5(rgyud): thugs rje chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i byin gyis brlabs dang / de mchi
2a1(rgyud): gi ye shes rnam pasna tshogs kyi khyad pa dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rin po che'i rabu rgyan gyis
2a2(rgyud): khams gsum gyi chos kyi rgyal po dbang bster ba mang 'a ba rnyes pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes na
2a3(rgyud): 'byor chen po'i dbang phyug/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya thams cad mnyam pa nyid du thugs sa chud cing / thams cad kyi
2a4(rgyud): dgos pa mdzad pa nyid kyis/ sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa thams cad kyi re ba yongs su baspong ba'i phrin pas mdzad pa/ 
2a5(rgyud): thugs rje kyi pa rnam par snang mdza dus gsul du gag par 'azhugs shing / sgra dang gsu dang / thugs thams cadang rje sa bung gyur pa'i de na
2b1(rgyud): shing dril bu btags pa/ dang dang 'bar dang / me tog gi phreng ba dang / rngam dang / dra ba dang dra ba phyed pa dang / zla ba rlung gis bskyod pa rnams kyis mdzes par byas par 'on na bya 'i rgyal pa 'oganas na
2b2(rgyud): dbyang chub sems dpa' bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgu la 'di la ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyogan rdo rje dang / kun tu spyan ngas gzigs kyi dbang po dang / nam mkha'i snying po dang / rdo rje khu gyu
2b3(rgyud): dang / 'jam dpal dang / sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / nam mkha'i mdzod dang / bdud kyi stobs thams cad rab tu 'joms pa la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
2b4(rgyud): ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgu dang / gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs te/ de lang 'di ltar 'dzam bu'i gling na de bzhin gshegs pa tshad med grangs med pa de dag gi
2b5(rgyud): skus kyang til gyi gang bu bzhin du gang bar snang ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku re re las kyang sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med tshad med pa rnams snang ngo // sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag na yang chos kyi tshul 'di dag 'chang
2b6(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad chen po/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad bzhin du rtag par bzhugs shing sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje lta bur gyur pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang
2b7(rgyud): ma pa nyid du 'jug pas/ rdo rje dbyings thams cad thugs su chud pa'i ye shes sems dpa' nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo rdo rje'i byin gyis brlabs las byung ba'i ye shes kyi snying po// 
2b8(rgyud): shegs pa mtha' yas pa nyid kyi rdo rje chen po'i ye shes rin po che'i dbang bskur ba'i rin po che chen po// nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du spros pa'i de bzhin nyid kyi ye shes mngon par rdzogs par byang
3a1(rgyud): chubabs/ byang chub bar thar bye / de bzhin gshegs pa thams ca nyid gang 'bye chos thams cad kyimang can dag par grags chud/ 
3a2(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi mga' da kyi don yod par ma da nyid kyis thams ca dang mnyam pa zed ci da med pa'iphrin las thams ca dpa da/  gshegs pa ngas pa kyi
3a3(rgyud): tshan rgya da/ de sa das/ rna kyi sa ga sa ge na / de ga
3a4(rgyud): thams cad kyis legs so sa kyi ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rin po che'i dbang chen po bsar ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams
3a5(rgyud): gshegs bya ba da kyibasam rgyal po na dzi bal ban dag shegs sa du len pa dang zhi gshegs pa
3a6(rgyud): da ni bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdod miza par thams cad kyi dgongos pa mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rkyen 'gru
3b1(rgyud): bathams cad kyi ba srung zhing bskyab pa'i gnod sbyin dang / de bzhir gshegs pa thams cad kyi skad nasung dang thugs rdo rje'i phyag rgya bcings pa'i ye shes rnams so// kun bzang rab tu gdon meg// bdu
3b2(rgyud): dgyes gtso bo dang // mkhab sgos shin tug tshon dang // rin chen dpal dang 'dzum pa che// kun tu gzigs dzin mtshan dang // 'jam dpa la dkyil le 'o thams cad da pa
3b3(rgyud): brtson 'grus ma rungs dam du gzung // rdo rje lcags kyu mda' gzhu dang // rin chen nyi ma rgyal mtshan 'dzum// pad ma ral gri 'khom lo gsum/ las dang so cha 'jigs byed bcings// thog ma tha
3b4(rgyud): marungs khro bo bzod pa che// gnod srin srin po dam pa brtan// gze chen dpa' bo dbang po ma// yu ma'i bdag po skye dgu'i mgon// gtogs 'dod rgyal 'dod thub pa che// 'jig rten stong dang mkha' dngas
3b5(rgyud): 'jig rte gsum dang khams gsum pa// 'bang chen sems cad don rab mdzad// thams cad dgu la tshangs pa dang // 'khor dang mya ngang 'da' dang rtag/ kha da 'tsho dang mchod pa che// sangs rgyas dag pa theg pa che// 
3b6(rgyud): srid gsum rtag pabang de yin no// 'jug rten gsum rgya ba byed spyod dang // bde spyod gtso bo 'dul ma nga// rdo rje gcod nga ma rab mchog/ ye shes pa rol phyin pa'i tshul// byang chub sems dpa'i
3b7(rgyud): 'ang // de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi spyod/ sangs myasadon dang sangs rgyas thugs// byang chub kun da thun med// rnam par snang ma myal phyi ga s+ho/ dbyung gzungs dang dran pa dang / sems
3b8(rgyud): lal mdzad// yang dag sangs rgyas kun bdag nyid// yod pa rtag dod rtogs mdzad pa// sdong po chen po nag pa tsho// 'dod chags chen po 'deb che// thabs tshe
4a1(rgyud): mchog chen mchog/ kun gyi mchog dang gnas dbang ga/ bcom ldan byang chub dran pa'i thugs// byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po ni de bzhin gshegs
4a2(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi thugs la gnas so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di dper na til gyi gang bu bzhin du yongs su gang bar gyur to// de nas de bzhin gsheg
4a3(rgyud): pa thams cad 'dus te byang chub sems dpa' chen po don thams cad grub pa zhes bya ba byang chub kyi snying por bzhugs pa gang na ba der gshegs te/ byang chub sems dpa' de la ched du rdzogs pa
4a4(rgyud): longs spyod pa'i sku bstan nas 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu khyod kyis gang gi phyir de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de kho na nyid mngon par ma rtogs par dka' ba spyod pa thams cad la spro ba
4a5(rgyud): skyed cing / ji ltar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par bya snyam/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po don thams cad grub pa/ de bzhin gshegs paH
4a6(rgyud): dkyis bskul bas mi g.yo ba'i ting nge 'dzin de las bzhengs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams
4a7(rgyud): rlom na pa gas/ de myu na ba sgrub pa kyi sngam padags ga de sad sa gsol pa bzhin gshegs pa dug pa sna kyi gas cig di skad kyis ka'/ 
4a8(rgyud): gi la to// me nyam pa gas tshan rigs da slo gi rnal gyi gas sa kyi rlo na / don kyi mam
4b1(rgyud): cad grub pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'deskad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams bdag gi ste gran bya ba'i dkyi 'kho lngabu gda'ab bdag gis rtogs / 
4b2(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa rigs kyi bu sems de ni rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal bas sa da ni'i lteng sbyangs bde ltar gyur te/ de' napas dag tsho tshon gyis bsgyur ba bzhin no// den
4b3(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'i sems shes pa rgyas par bya ba'i phyir/ oM bo d+hi NeH udz+nyo ta bA mi zhes bya ba rang bzhin gyis grub pa'i sngags 'dis/ yang byang chub se
4b4(rgyud): dpa' chen po de'i sems bskyed par gyur to// de nas yang byang chub sems dpa' des/ de bzhino gshogs pa thams cad rtsol bkas byang chub kyi sems bskyed nas 'di skad ces gsol to// zla ba'i dkyi
4b5(rgyud): 'khor lta bur mthong ba gang legs pa de ni zla ba'i dkyil 'khor nyid du mthong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po sems bskyed pa kun tu
4b6(rgyud): gabo khyod kyis mngon sum du myur gyis/ de legs par bsgrungs shig/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sems bskyed pa kun tu bzang po de brtan par bya ba'i phyir/ sngags 'dis rang gi snying gar zla ba
4b7(rgyud): dkyil 'khor la rdo rje'i dbyibs su soms shig/ oM ting badz+ra/ byang chub sems dpas gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi steng du rdo rje 'dug par bdag gi
4b8(rgyud): / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa/ de di gshegs pa thams cad kyi ru dub po semasadze rje de sngags 'dis brta par gyis shig/ oM bkres hAgo
5a1(rgyud): de nas nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du mnyam par 'jug pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje dngas ji snyed pa de dag
5a2(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin brlabs kyis sems dpa'i rdo rje der zhugs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' chen po don thams
5a3(rgyud): dbyings zhes bya ba'i ming gis dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje dbyings kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad la 'di skad ces gso
5a4(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi d+harma'i spu ni bdag legs par mthong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa/ se
5a5(rgyud): dpa' chen po de lta bas na/ sems dpa'i rdo rje de rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi skung bdag nyid rang bzhin gyis grub pa'i sngags ci dga' bar zlos la sgoms shig/ oM la bsan
5a6(rgyud): tathA ga ta tas+tha a haM/ de nas de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i dbyings kyis bdag nyid de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas/ de nas de
5a7(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad la phyag byas te 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bdag sprin gyis rlobs pa mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i da btad
5a8(rgyud): / de des de na chos gsol pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdo rje dbyings kyi sems pa'i da rje da bugs so// de das bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
5b1(rgyud): sa kyis nad ma /  dag shegs pa thams coM 'an pa pardzogs pas sa rgyas so// ngakunan gshegs pa mams da
5b2(rgyud): be shes kyi phyag tu gsang ba'i dmatshig zhuzhugs so// debyizhi na gshegs pa thams cad kyi rje chen po tshe'i dbang bsrung ba mnyam pa nyid kyi shes kyi phyag rgya gsang pa'i dam cig tu zhugs so// de bzhin
5b3(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes rtogs pa rang bzhin gyis dag go/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thams cad mnyam pa nyid rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal zhing ye shes kyi 'byung
5b4(rgyud): gnas su gyur pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su gyur to// de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sems dpa'i rdo rje de las de bzhin gshegs pa
5b5(rgyud): dbyang nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes bskyed/ nam mkha' las byung ba'i nor bu rin po che chen po'i dbang bskur bas dbang bskur ro// kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyis
5b6(rgyud): chos kyi ye shes bskyed/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phrin las thams cad la ban gnas/ ri rab kyi rtse me gang na ba dang / khang bu 'artsegs pa rtse mo rdo rje nar bu dang rin po che las byas pa gang na bder
5b7(rgyud): gshegs te byon nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje dbyings de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad du byin gyis brlabs nas dbyer med par gyur te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi seng ge'i gdan 'an pa
5b8(rgyud): stan te bzhugs par gyur to// na sa de bzhin gshegs pa mi bskyod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen 'byung ldan dang / de bzhin gshegs pa sman ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i rgyal po dang / de bzhin
6a1(rgyud): gshegs pa gdod ma thab dgrub pa rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dusas nas bdag nyid kyis byan rgyas brlabs te/ bcom ldan 'das shA thub pa nan
6a2(rgyud): ba thams cad mnyam pa nyid du rab tu rtog pa'i phyir phyogs thams cad mnyam pa nyid du dmigs nas phyogs bzhir bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad de bzhin gshegs pa ma
6a3(rgyud): par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas ring po ma lon pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi nam mkha' las byung ba'i nor bu rin po
6a4(rgyud): popo'i dbang gis dbang bskur ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i chos kyi ye shes dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kying
6a5(rgyud): / las thams cad gdon mi za bar ston pa/ thogs pa med pa/ dgongs pa rdzogs pa/ yid kyi bsam pa'o cog yongs su rdzogs pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad du bdag nyid kyis byin gyis brlabs nas
6a6(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba'i dam tshig las byung ba/ sems dpa'i byin gyis brlabs pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting ngange 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs
6a7(rgyud): bani gshegs pa thams cad kyi theg pa chen po mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di/ rang gi thugs gnas phyung ngo // badz+ra satwa/ de nas de bzhid gshegs
6a8(rgyud): 'thams cad kyi thugs ka nas byung ma thagapa 'de de/ bcom ldan 'das kun tu babang pod nyid pa'i'i dkyil 'khor du gyur nas byung ste/ sems can thams cad kyi byang chub kyi sems chen po yang dag
6b1(rgyud): ngas nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyogs phyogs su la khyad do// de nas bla ba la kyilal por de dag las kyang de 'di gshegs pathams cad kyi ye shes kyi rdo rje byung ste/ bcom ldan 'ad
6b2(rgyud): raMny+dza mdzad de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs su thugs par gyur ro// rdo rje sems depa'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu brtan pa dang / de dan gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis gcig tu
6b3(rgyud): par gyur nas nam mkha'i khams thams cad du 'od zer rtse lnga pa'i phreng bas khyab par zhugs te de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje lta bu'i dbyings su gyur nas/ de ba
6b4(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs ka nas byung ste phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje de las rdo rje de lta bu'i 'od zer gzugs dang kha dog sa tshogs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du snga
6b5(rgyud): khyab par byed pa rnams byung ngo // rdo rje lta bu'i 'od zer de dag gi rtsem pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rngub shin tu phra mo snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis byung ste chos kyi dbyings kun tu khyab pa
6b6(rgyud): thams cad dang / nam mokha'i khams kyi mthas gtugs pa thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rab 'bram rgya mtsho'i sprin thams cad du bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes mngon
6b7(rgyud): par byang chub pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub kyi sems chen po'i rnyed pa dang / kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa sna tshogs pa bslab pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs mnyes par mdzad pa dang / byang
6b8(rgyud): rab kye snying po chen por gshegs pa dang bdud thams cad 'dul ba dang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyim pa nyid kyi byeng chub chen por mngon par byang chub pa dang dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bkod ba nas
7a1(rgyud): bsad sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnams yongs su sub cing thams cad la ngan pa dang bdab yangad pa dang da bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye gas
7a2(rgyud): dang mngon par shes pa dam pa'i dngos grub bsgrub pa la sogs pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang po tshul rnams kyi bar du bsten nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzid ni kun tu bzang po yin
7a3(rgyud): ba dang / shin tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun du bzang po'i skur sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs pa gnas nas/ 'di skad du che
7a4(rgyud): du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma'o bdag ni rang byung ba'i// kun tu bzang po sems dpa' brtan// de ni btAn phyir lus min yang // sems dpa'i lus su gyur ba yin// de nas byang chub sems
7a5(rgyud): dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po'i sku/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs ka nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyan sngan zla ba'i dkyil la ro la gnas nas/ bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas
7a6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ting nge 'dzin dang ye shes kyi dam tshig rdorje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi tshul khrims dang ting nge
7a7(rgyud): don dang shes rab dang / rnam par grol ba dang rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba dang chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang sems can gyi don bya ba dang thabs chen po dang / stobs dang brtson 'grus dang ye shes chen
7a8(rgyud): po'i dam tshig dang sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnams yongs su bsab pa dang thams cad kyi dbang por bya ba dang / thams cad kyi
7b1(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes dang mngon par shes pa blan pad pa dang / theg pa can pa mngan par rtogs pa grub pa'i mchog pa pa' bar du/ 'bras bu de dag gi byarang byang chub sems dpa' sems
7b2(rgyud): rin po kun na banang pod/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo sbyor ba nyid du sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sgra rin po che'i dbu rgyan dang rjod pan gyi dbang gis dbang bskur nas de bzhin gshegs pa thabs
7b3(rgyud): de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis/ lag na rdo rje lagan rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje'i ming gi dbang gis dbang skur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dang
7b4(rgyud): phyag g.yas pas rdo rje thugs kar gsor zhing 'phen pa'i tshul du li
7b5(rgyud): dablan med pa 'di// bdag ste bdag gi lag tu byin// rdo rje la ni rdo rje gnas/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gdon mi za bi'i rgyal po 'di tshig las byung ba'i
7b6(rgyud): / dpa'i byin gyis brlabs pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sman drang ba'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'darang
7b7(rgyud): thugs kanas phyung ngo // 'dra blang / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kanas byung ma zag pa 'di ni bcom ldan 'das phyag na rje nyid de/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi lugs mtshan po
7b8(rgyud): byung nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang bad kyi thugs su zhugs te gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje lcags cu chen po'i dbyings su gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag gnyis su gnas so// den
8a1(rgyud): rdo rje lugs kyu'i dbyangs char pad las ngag tan gyi khabs thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mod mnyam pa rang nad gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung / de na dgas
8a2(rgyud): thams cad kun drang ba la sogs pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi du 'phrul dang rdzu 'phrul rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge ridzin ni shin tu gdon mi za ba'i rgyal po yin pa dang / shin tu na
8a3(rgyud): rer gcig tu 'dres par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po gdon mi za bi'i lus su gud nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang ma rad kyi thugs la gnas te ched du brjod pa 'di ched du
8a4(rgyud): rje las byung ba'i/ lcags kya nges pa'i rgyal po bdag/ gang phye kun tu rangs rgyas khyab// rdung phyer kun nas spyan 'dred to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shin tu ga me/ 
8a5(rgyud): 'argyal po'i sgra bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs ka nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi g.yas phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas /
